### B704 вҖ” 1-ft labeled contour lines, client-generated from the raw 3DEP DEM in a Web Worker `[Site Planner / GIS]` (feature) #site-planner #gis #perf  *(owner brief 2026-07-07, arrived as "NEW-2"; **B704** = B703 + 1. Branch `claude/elevation-houston-relief-7co7do`.)*
`[x]` **IMPLEMENTED + headless-verified this session; parks (Verify: live вҖ” GIS endpoint + zoom-/data-density-dependent rendering classes) вҶ’ V240.**
- Verify: live
- Origin: filed 2026-07-07 from chat
- **Why client-side:** the public service's canned contour renderings are raster-only, unlabeled, and (at best preset) 2-ft вҖ” no labeled 1-ft vector lines exist server-side. The raw grid path was probe-verified first: `exportImage?format=lerc&pixelType=F32&renderingRule=None` returns LERC1 (`CntZImage`), decoded with the official `lerc` npm package; a real Katy tile is committed as `test/fixtures/dep-katy-463x400.lerc` (463Г—400 F32, 120.9вҖ“149.8 ft вҖ” drives the decode-contract tests without network).
- **What shipped (new deps: `lerc` + `d3-contour`, both small вҖ” the two the brief authorized):**
  - **Pure core** (`lib/demGrid.js`, `lib/contours.js`): deterministic snapped-tile grid requests (key вҶ” bbox bijection; smoothing margin baked in; oversized viewports coarsen deterministically; `adjustAspectRatio=false` + size computed to match the bbox aspect exactly вҖ” a silently adjusted bbox would shift every contour, and a size mismatch on decode REFUSES loudly); LERC magic-byte sniff (the dev server SPA-fallbacks `/api/*` to index.html вҖ” "response arrived" вү  "response is a grid"); meters вҶ’ survey-ft on decode (`M_TO_FT` now exported from `elevation.js` вҖ” one conversion for every 3DEP consumer); normalized MASKED gaussian smooth (voids never bleed; unsmoothed 1-ft contours from Вұ0.1вҖ“0.3 ft LiDAR noise are jagged spaghetti); marching squares via `d3-contour` with **sentinel-embedded voids** (never NaN вҖ” d3's smoothing emits NaN coords and Leaflet throws) and **two strip passes** (grid-border frame + dilated-void halo, so lines BREAK at water instead of bridging or outlining it); pixel-space DouglasвҖ“Peucker (the newly exported `vectorLayers.douglasPeucker`; degree-space tolerance is anisotropic on the ground); index flag every 5 ft; sparse labels capped ~30.
  - **The repo's first Web Worker** (`lib/terrainWorker.js`, Vite `?worker`): decode/smooth/trace off the main thread; import list pinned by `test/terrainWorker.test.js` (a Leaflet/DOM import would crash at worker RUNTIME, not build time); the raw grid transfers back for the B706 readout.
  - **Leaflet glue** (`lib/terrainLayers.js`): overpass-pattern view-driven layerGroup (moveend refresh, B56d busy/pending trailing edge, `gisCache.swr` last-good painting with data age) with the terrain specifics вҖ” fetch on the MAIN thread (gisCache is localStorage-bound; proxyвҶ’direct one-shot fallback mirrors wireRaster), ONE deduped fetch+compute per tile shared with B705 and the readout, grids in a small LRU Map (a Float32Array must never ride `gisCache.write` вҖ” it JSON.stringifies unconditionally), canvas-renderer polylines (`interactive:false`; hierarchy by WEIGHT per the salience rule), white-halo divIcon labels, restyle-in-place `setOpacity`, worker-crash lazy rebuild.
  - **Registry** (`lib/layers.js`): `TERRAIN.contours` ("Contour lines (1 ft)"), `kind: "contours"` dispatch, vintage row; both surfaces pick it up automatically. **Zoom-gated вүҘ 16** (honesty: at z15 a capped grid is ~6 m cells вҖ” 1-ft contours would be mush).
  - **Calibration:** the ramp test pins d3-contour's smoothed output to the cell-center convention (measured: level 20 of an x-ramp lands at exactly px 20.5), so contours, the hover readout, and the cross-section tool can never disagree by half a cell. Elevations are NAVD88 orthometric вҖ” the same vertical datum FEMA BFEs use (stated in the layer note; relevant to the future FFE-vs-BFE feature).
- **Verified here (sandbox):** 60+ new unit tests across the `demGrid`/`contours`/`terrainWorker` suites (calibration, cone closed-ring, void break-not-bridge with halo assertion, masked-smooth void-bleed, fixture decode contract, artifact under the 512 KB cache cap) В· full suite green В· build green (worker chunk emits self-contained) В· headless: ONE LERC fetch, 30 halo labels painted, real canvas ink, vintage + caveat lines render.

- **What shipped:** `lib/flowField.js` (pure): downhill direction from a central-difference **gradient** over the harder-smoothed grid, windowed to the sample spacing вҖ” raw per-cell D8 at sparse samples reads as random 8-quantized noise on near-flat Houston terrain, so the gradient drives the ARROWS while **classic D8 is kept alongside, pure, as the seed of the future storm-outfall flow-accumulation feature** (extend D8 вҶ’ accumulation to answer "which outfall does this part of the site drain to" вҖ” the B641-adjacent note the brief asked recorded). Screen-spaced lattice (~70 px); arrow length + weight scale with slope (bolder = steeper вҖ” salience tracks importance); slope computed in ft/ft with the cos(lat) mercatorвҶ’ground correction (~0.868 at Houston вҖ” mercator meters overstate ground distance ~15%). **Flat/ambiguous/void samples get NO arrow** вҖ” never invent a direction (the no-auto-guess principle). Rides B704's tile end-to-end: NO second DEM fetch path (the same worker job computes both artifacts). Sign-convention unit tests pin east-falling вҶ’ east arrows and south-falling вҶ’ down-screen arrows (grid y-down vs latitude-up is the classic silent bug вҖ” uphill arrows pass every other test).

- **What shipped:**
  - The **whole pane is the drop target**, driven by a dragenter/dragleave **depth counter** (the old naive `currentTarget === target` dragleave flickered over children вҖ” the exact gotcha the brief flagged).
  - **Drag onto a folder row** in the left rail highlights it (dashed accent) and drops file straight into that folder; the "All files" row is the drop-to-auto-sort target; the drop-overlay pill names the REAL target (hovered row > selected folder > auto-file).

An explicit target (row drop / selected folder) still wins for the whole drop (B686/B687 semantics); a drop before the tree rows load falls back to classic auto-file (no empty-tree needs-filing dump); a drag cancelled outside the window resets the pane highlight (window dragend/drop/leave self-heal); rail navigation and the queue's Triage button clear an active search so a click never looks dead. The entry-API walk now stamps `relPath` (`uploadQueue.entryToFiles`); `webkitdirectory` picks already carry `webkitRelativePath`. All ingestion still rides the ONE B260-descended queue (`makeQueueItems`/`runPool`) вҖ” no forked pipeline; the folder-note summary honestly reports kept / needs-filing / skipped counts.
- **Verified here (sandbox):** unit tests (path-matcher ambiguity + contradiction rules, relPath stamping) В· full suite green В· build green В· logged-out headless smoke.
- **рҹ”Қ Adversarially reviewed (2026-07-07, 4 dimensions Г— verify): confirmed findings all fixed same-session** вҖ” the cross-branch unique-label guess (HIGH вҶ’ the contradiction guard above), the container-name mass-file (container excluded from routing), a LOWERCASED folder label stamped as the discipline corrupting doc-class/category (labels now case-preserved + normalized onto the canonical discipline list), row-hop highlight flicker (targets now arm on dragenter), a depth-counter desync pinning the overlay after an out-of-window release (window-dragleave self-heal), the folderRows-empty race, over-promising drop copy (the empty state + overlay pill now name the REAL target), and dead-feeling clicks with a search active (rail clicks / Triage clear the query; typing exits the holding view).

### B694 вҖ” County / city / ETJ boundary layers ride the cached vector tier: instant paint, no 503 stalls `[Site Planner / GIS]` (feature вҖ” amends B96, touches B176/B287) #site-planner #gis #perf  *(owner brief 2026-07-07, arrived as "NEW-2"; minted **B694**. - **AUDIT-FIRST correction to the brief:** the brief said the vector tier "already shipped for FEMA/NWI" вҖ” in fact `lib/vectorLayers.js` was UNWIRED groundwork (its only consumer was its own test; the earlier `vectorOverlay.js` had been deleted as unwired, and FEMA/NWI render via the raster f=image path to this day). Engine additions (`lib/vectorLayers.js`, all pure + unit-tested): **detail tiers** (`pickTier`) with **server-side generalization** (`maxAllowableOffset` вҖ” the agency thins vertices before the wire, replacing client DouglasвҖ“Peucker for tiered pulls, which is the brief's per-zoom simplify done cheaper), tier-stamped cache keys (`vectorKey`), and **outward grid-snap** (`snapBbox`) so pans reuse entries.
- **Cache design (measured live 2026-07-07 via curl):** county coarse tier = ONE statewide source-level entry (`vec:jur_county:all@0.002`, 254 counties, **337 KB** @0.002В° вүҲ 200 m вҖ” fits the 512 KB `maxEntryBytes` cap, so no per-county split; the brief's open question, answered empirically); ETJ coarse = one H-GAC-region entry (608 features, **204 KB** @0.001В°); city is always bbox-scoped (statewide too heavy; a metro cell вүҲ **120 KB**). Fine tiers (zвүҘ12/13) are bbox-scoped @0.0002В° on a snap grid. TTLs: county 30 d, city/ETJ 14 d (annexations/SB2038 move these occasionally; SWR shows age either way). Per B96's own note, the **refreshed-age stamp folded into the B236 vintage line** вҖ” one surface: `as of: <vintage> В· refreshed <age> (updatingвҖҰ)`, stale in `--warn-text` (the standalone age chip is gone).
- **Never-blank fallback (the decideVectorOrImage intent, adapted):** boundaries are always-vector (no image service exists) вҖ” `minVectorZoom:0`/`maxAreaDeg:вҲһ` so no gate can flip them; a **failed pull with nothing cached** engages the injected live fallback = the previous esri-leaflet `featureLayer` path **with its B287 retry/backoff**, LOUD through the same status channel (`liveFallback`, dependency-injected from `layers.js` so `vectorOverlay` stays esri-leaflet-free). A cold-cache fetch failure now THROWS in `fetchCached` instead of resolving a silent null (LOUD-FAILURE). B176 invariant preserved: same `GIS_SOURCES` endpoints as the jurisdiction identify вҖ” the line you see is the line the identify reports.
- **Verified here (sandbox):** 48 vectorLayers unit tests (tiers/snap/keys/onFresh/cold-throw/registry) + headless with a seeded cache + the TxDOT host BLOCKED: boundaries painted in **~50 ms with zero network**, one statewide cache entry (`vec:jur_county:all@0.002p4`), folded age line rendering, toggle-off clears clean, zero page errors. The correctly-shaped statewide query (no envelope + `maxAllowableOffset=0.002`) observed leaving the browser before the sandbox proxy reset it вҖ” the live leg is V234.
- **рҹ”Қ Adversarially reviewed (2026-07-07, 4 dimensions; verify agents hit the session token cap so every finding was verified BY HAND against the code): 18 raw findings вҶ’ 10 root causes confirmed, all fixed same-session.** The theme: the overlay's race guards and the fallback's honesty. Fixed: (1) `engageFallback` + the zoom-gate branch now bump the request `seq` вҖ” an in-flight fetch can no longer paint stale vectors OVER the live fallback or BELOW the zoom gate; (2) a SUPERSEDED request's failure no longer latches `lastVectorError` (and a successful pull clears it) вҖ” a mid-pan blip can't permanently downgrade the layer to the fallback; (3) the fallback layer gets the `setOpacity` shim esri-leaflet FeatureLayers lack (the opacity slider was dead after engagement) and reports "loading", not a false-healthy "loaded", right after the failure that engaged it; (4) the basemap status dot keys off `tileload` вҖ” Leaflet fires layer-`load` even when EVERY tile errored, which showed green over a gray canvas; (5) a DFW-scale city cell measured **560 KB stored** (over the 512 KB cap вҶ’ silent L1-only) вҖ” the widest city tier now thins at 0.003В°/3 dp with a mid tier at z11вҖ“12; (6) cache keys stamp `precision` too (`@0.002p4`) so a registry retune busts the cache instead of serving old-detail geometry for a TTL; (7) the identify popover closes on toggle-off/fallback (it used to outlive the layer); (8) a FAILED background refresh clears `lastKey` so the next map move retries (was: "(updatingвҖҰ)" forever with no retry); (9) cold pulls no longer paint twice (swr's cold-fetch `onFresh` is skipped via the `lastKey` guard); (10) select mode neutralizes the interactive fill's `cursor:pointer` (`.pf-select-mode` + `pf-boundary-hit`, index.css) so the +/вҲ’ parcel cursor survives вҖ” B98 extends to the cursor. **Accepted as documented limitations:** gisCache's oldest-write-first eviction could recycle the standing statewide entry under a full 3 MB namespace (a later re-pull, not a failure вҖ” changing B96's shared eviction policy would touch the identify/overpass consumers), and an over-cap entry staying L1-only is graceful degradation by design.
> **Dedup:** consumes B96's cache exactly as it anticipated; keeps B287's retry as the fallback leg; does NOT collide with B371 (analysis-side offline pre-cache, still Later) or B629 (parcels).

### B692 вҖ” ROOT-CAUSE fix for the B690 husk-parcel crash: sanitize the model funnel so a null/points-less entry can never be manufactured, persisted, or re-ingested `[Site Planner / model]` (bug вҖ” CRITICAL, owner-reported crash; extends B690) #site-planner #persistence  *(owner chat 2026-07-07 вҖ” incognito tab on planyr.io: "Site Planyr hit an error and couldn't loadвҖҰ Try again/Reload/Ctrl-Shift-R all send me right back." Branch `claude/site-planner-incognito-error-49h3as`. DEDUPE-FIRST вҖ” same crash as **B690** (both symbolicated to `ymвҶ’HpвҶ’Ij`), so this item is deliberately the ROOT-CAUSE COMPANION, not a duplicate: B690 guarded the reads; B692 stops the husk from ever existing вҖ” manufacture (normalizeZ), persistence (createSiteModel funnel), and every ingress (rows, realtime, JSON import) вҖ” and makes sanitization LOUD.)*
`[x]` **IMPLEMENTED + fully repro'd/verified headless this session; parks in вҸі Verify (Verify: live вҖ” the repro cites the owner's real signed-in data; the signed-in mirror path + the telemetry signal need a live confirmation) вҶ’ V232.**
- Verify: live
- Origin: filed 2026-07-07 from chat (crash 2026-07-07 02:23вҖ“02:30 UTC, 23 telemetry reports, build dca4f15, all signed-in)
- **Root cause (found via the app's own `client_errors` telemetry вҖ” minified stack symbolicated against the deployed chunk):** `MapFinder.siteAcres` reduces `shoelace(p.points)` over `site.parcels`, guarded on the ARRAY but not the ENTRY. A `null` entry in a persisted parcels array (JSON.stringify turns an `undefined` entry or an array hole into `null`) survived `createSiteModel` untouched, and B671's `normalizeZ` then spread it into a `{z:0}` "husk" with no points вҖ” `undefined.length` вҶ’ the workspace error boundary, on EVERY load, because the poison lives in the stored record. Cloud DB swept clean (site_elements + sites blobs, all users) вҖ” the husk was client-manufactured into the local mirror during the element-sync churn window (RLS-rejected commit 01:30 + create collisions + a two-tab CAS heal loop 01:33вҖ“02:03).
- **Fix (funnel + belt-and-suspenders):** (1) `createSiteModel` now DROPS non-object entries from every collection (parcels/els/markups/measures/callouts/sheetOverlays/parcelDrawings/crossSections) and drops points-less husk parcels вҖ” reference-stable when clean, so no state/save churn; runs before `migrateRoads` so a null can't crash the els migration passes either. (2) `normalizeZ`/`needsZ` never spread a non-object into a `{z}` husk (drop instead). (3) `MapFinder.shoelace` returns 0 for a non-array (the list can never crash on residual junk). (4) The rows-read paths (`refetchReplace` + realtime `applyRemoteInstr`) keep husk parcel rows OFF the canvas; the reconcile diff then tombstones the bad row in the cloud вҖ” the husk heals into a proper delete (TOMBSTONE-DELETES). (4b) The JSON-import path now normalizes through `createSiteModel` (was raw `setParcels(d.parcels)`) вҖ” a hand-edited/stale export can't re-poison the canvas (found by the parallel writer-hunt audit; the audit also confirmed via DB sweep that NO other user has husk data and no one else was affected). (5) LOUD-FAILURE: `loadSitesList` reports a `model-sanitized` telemetry event whenever a stored record needed junk dropped вҖ” corruption is a visible signal, never a quiet edit. Bonus: the e2e fixture generator's parcel used `ring:` instead of `points:` (a real husk shipping in the fixture) вҖ” fixed + fixtures/goldens regenerated.
- **Self-heal:** no user action вҖ” the poisoned record reads clean on the next load (drop-at-read), and the next save persists the cleaned model.
- **Tests/verify (sandbox):** 2,875 green (11 new in `test/modelSanitize.test.js`: husk manufacture, per-collection drops, reference stability, idempotence, junk counting) В· build green В· **controlled repro BOTH ways headless (`ui-audit/verify-husk-parcel.mjs`): the poisoned seed CRASHES live planyr.io with the owner's exact error, and renders clean (site listed, correct 23.0 ac from the surviving parcel) on the fixed build.**

Rings auto-closed (first vertex = last); `<innerBoundaryIs>` holes supported at the format layer; placemark `<name>` from the layer label / building number / parcel address.
- **3D massing (enhancement):** "Export with 3D buildings" extrudes each building to its clear height (`<extrude>1</extrude>` + `relativeToGround` + per-vertex altitude in metres); flat `clampToGround` is the default and the fallback when height is unknown.
- **LOUD-FAILURE:** `siteToFeatures` THROWS if any vertex reprojects to a non-finite number вҶ’ the caller (`flashWarn` on the canvas, `setErr` on the map) aborts loudly, never a partial/misregistered file. Empty site вҶ’ "nothing to export" (no empty file); a plan with no geo anchor вҶ’ blocked with a plain-English hint. Names XML-escaped; download filename sanitized. Local download only (default-private; no sharing surface).
- **Two entry points:** map viewer right-click on empty map вҶ’ exports every visible site (honoring the status-chip filter), each as its own folder, + any selected parcels; canvas right-click on empty space вҶ’ exports the open plan.

Full suite green В· lint 0 errors В· build green.

### B682 вҖ” Dragging a parcel's acreage label spawns a "bunch of copies" (id-less parcels + value-based union merge) `[Site Planner]` (bug) #site-planner #persistence #selection  *(owner chat 2026-07-06 вҖ” screenshot: "I just tried to move the 69.48 ac label, and it just made a bunch of copies." **B682** = highest real B# across both files (B681) + 1. Branch `claude/acre-label-duplication-ulvjys`. DEDUPE-FIRST вҖ” grepped Open/вҸі Verify/Done for `acre`/`label`/`parcel` Г— `dup`/`copies`: NOT B651 (split double-COUNTS acreage in the yield math вҖ” different defect, same area), NOT B22 (rapid-click duplicate SELECTION on the map). Net-new: the parcel-identity/merge defect.)*
`[x]` **IMPLEMENTED + sandbox-verified + headless-verified this session; parks in вҸі Verify (Verify: live вҖ” the accumulation is a concurrency/multi-writer MERGE class per LIVE-VERIFY, only fully exercised signed-in over cloud sync) вҶ’ V225.**
- Verify: live
- Origin: filed 2026-07-06 from chat
- **AUDIT-FIRST root cause:** map-finder / legacy parcels can be **id-LESS**. `MapFinder.computeAssembly` emits `{points, addr, acct, attrs}` with **no `id`** (the modern `newSiteFromMap` backfills one, but records created before that вҖ” or synced from an older client вҖ” still hold id-less parcels). Two bugs flow from a missing id: (1) the acreage-chip drag matches `pc.id === draggedId`, and with both `undefined` it moves EVERY id-less parcel at once; (2) the cross-copy union merge (`mergeSiteContent` вҶ’ `unionById`) can only dedupe id-less items by **`JSON.stringify` value**, so the instant a drag adds a `labelOffset` the edited copy no longer equals its stored twin and the union keeps **BOTH** вҖ” a phantom parcel that **multiplies** with each further drag/merge. Proven with a focused `mergeSiteContent` repro (1 id-less parcel + a labelOffset edit вҶ’ **2** parcels).
- **Fix (one funnel, additive):** `createSiteModel` вҖ” which every load/save/merge passes through вҖ” now backfills a **deterministic id derived from the parcel GEOMETRY only** (`withStableParcelIds`, djb2-xor over rounded points), so the same parcel hashes identically before/after any mutable-field edit (labelOffset/active/locked/setbacks) and the union dedupes it by id; two genuinely-distinct parcels differ in points вҶ’ distinct ids. Only fills a MISSING id (in-planner parcels keep their `uid()`), idempotent + reference-stable on already-migrated data. Exact-geometry id-less duplicates collapse to one, which **self-heals the phantom copies the bug already persisted** on the next load. No change needed in `SitePlanner.jsx` вҖ” parcels reaching React state now always carry an id, so the chip drag matches exactly one.
- **Verified here (sandbox):** 6 new unit tests in `test/siteModel.test.js` (backfill determinism В· geometry-only stability across a labelOffset edit В· distinct-geometry distinct ids В· existing id never rewritten В· the merge repro now yields 1 not 2 В· exact-dup self-heal) В· full suite **2,788 green** В· lint 0 errors В· build green.
- **Verified here (headless, logged-out):** seeded a site with 3 id-less parcels (2 exact-geometry dupes, one carrying a dragged `labelOffset`, + 1 distinct), opened it in the real plan canvas вҶ’ exactly **2** acre chips render (dupe collapsed, distinct survived), zero page errors. (Temp spec, removed after the run вҖ” the unit tests are the durable guard.)
- **вҸі V225** = the signed-in / cloud pass: on a real account whose project has (or is seeded with) id-less parcels, drag an acreage label repeatedly across cloud syncs / a second tab and confirm it stays put with NO new copies, and that any pre-existing phantom copies collapse on load.

### B669 вҖ” Keep-alive module switching: visited workspaces stay mounted (hidden), switching is instant `[Shell / all modules]` (feature вҖ” owner request) #ui #perf #infra  *(owner chat 2026-07-05 вҖ” "it should be a cleaner switch between clicking on modulesвҖҰ it's almost like we start from nothing"; **B669** = highest real B# across both files (B668) + 1. ### B667 вҖ” Review remembers the last document PER PROJECT (+ the resume self-clobber fix) `[Doc Review]` (feature + bug вҖ” owner request) #doc-review #persistence  *(owner chat 2026-07-05 вҖ” "whatever I last reviewed, what the last document that I reviewed in that project should stay open too"; **B667** = B666 + 1. `[x]` **IMPLEMENTED this session; parks in вҸі Verify (Verify: live вҖ” resume needs signed-in cloud loads; timing class) вҶ’ V217.**
- Verify: live
- Origin: filed 2026-07-05 from chat
- **AUDIT-FIRST find вҖ” resume was self-clobbering (the real reason Review "started from nothing"):** the mount-time pointer writes (`lastSingleId` = this session's fresh blank id, `lastMode`="review") ran in declaration order BEFORE the boot effect read the keys back, so resume loaded a never-saved review and silently fell to the empty state on every reload. Same pattern in `Stitcher.jsx` (`lastStitchId`). Fixed structurally: the stored pointers are captured at FIRST RENDER (before any effect can write) and all pointer writes stay silent until boot resolves вҖ” no clobber window at all.
- **Per-project memory:** new map `planyr:docreview:lastDoc:v1` = `{ [projectId|""]: {id, mode} }` (`lib/lastDoc.js` вҖ” pure, 14 unit tests). Legacy globals keep being written and remain the fallback (migration = fallback, not a copy pass вҖ” existing devices resume day one). Boot resolves ordered candidates via `resolveResume` (URL project вҶ’ that project's own entry first, then legacy, still guarded by `wrongProject` on the actually-loaded record вҖ” a project-matched entry now RESUMES where the guard used to drop to empty). Breadcrumb project switch inside Review lands on THAT project's last doc (flushes the outgoing doc first; a pending cross-workspace open intent or an in-flight open wins вҖ” no race).
- **DEDUPE-FIRST:** no prior per-project-resume item (grepped `lastSingleId` В· `resume` В· `wrongProject`); B478 (resume-into-planner) is the Site-side analogue, different surface.
- **Verified here (sandbox):** `test/lastDoc.test.js` 14 green В· full suite green В· build green.
- **вҸі V217** = signed-in: open doc X in project A and doc Y in project B вҶ’ breadcrumb AвҶ”B resumes each project's own doc; reload a deep link `#/project/A/markup` reopens X; reload with an empty hash reopens the exact doc last on screen (also covers the B666 module+project restore chain end-to-end).

### B651 вҖ” Parcel split double-counts acreage; make split REPLACE the parent (parent + children can never both be active) `[Site Planner]` (bug) #site-planner #yield #selection  *(owner brief 2026-07-04, arrived as "NEW-1"; **B651** = highest real B# across both files (B650) + 1. Branch `claude/parcel-split-double-count-vk8f0j`. DEDUPE-FIRST вҖ” net-new: NOT B416 (Split-a-parcel discoverability / panel reachability, Done), NOT B128 (concave-cut split GEOMETRY, Done). Same feature area, different defect: those made the split tool reachable and its cut correct; this fixes what the split does to the parcel MODEL / active set.)*
`[x]` **IMPLEMENTED + headless-verified this session; parks in вҸі Verify (Verify: live вҖ” repro cites real project data) вҶ’ V210.** A split parcel and its children occupy the SAME ground, so any active set containing a parent AND a child double-counts that acreage (owner repro: Parcel 3, 16.40 ac вҶ’ 2.52 + 13.87 ac children, all three active вҶ’ Yield sums вүҲ 31.8 ac).
- Verify: live
- Origin: filed 2026-07-04 from chat
- **AUDIT-FIRST reconciliation (code reality vs. the report):** the current `performSplit` (`SitePlanner.jsx`, since PR #444 / #468) already **replaced + tombstoned** the parent, so the exact "split tool leaves all three active" no longer reproduces via the cut tool on `main`. The owner's live вүҲ31.8 ac most plausibly came from **overlapping county parcels added separately** (a recently-subdivided tract where CAD still lists the parent + both children) or a **stale cached bundle** predating that fix вҖ” which is exactly why **B652 (the overlap warning) is the real catch-all** and was built alongside. This item still had a genuine gap vs. the owner's desired UX (the old code DELETED the parent instead of retaining it), so the split was re-architected from "delete parent" to "supersede parent."
- **What shipped (branch `claude/parcel-split-double-count-vk8f0j`; lint 0 В· 2,526 tests (+21) В· build green В· lazy split intact В· headless `ui-audit/verify-b651-b652-parcel-split.mjs` 14/14):**
  - **Split is now a REPLACEMENT via supersession** (`performSplit`): one op creates + activates the pieces as CHILDREN (each carries `parentId`) and marks the parent `active:false` (superseded, non-counting) вҖ” no longer deleted/tombstoned. Because the superseded parent is inactive, it drops out of every active-parcel area sum automatically (no yield-math change needed; the ~13 inline `active !== false` sums are untouched).
  - **Parent retained + nested** (`parcelOutline` in `siteModel.js`; Parcel panel): the superseded parent stays in the list, greyed + "В· split", with its children indented under it. The **on-canvas** superseded outline is hidden (its active children occupy the same ground). Header "Parcels В· N" counts CURRENT lots only (excludes superseded), so splitting one lot reads "Parcels В· 2".
  - **Lineage naming** (`parcelDisplayInfo`, derived вҖ” not stored): Parcel 3 вҶ’ 3A / 3B вҶ’ 3A1 / 3A2 (letters odd depth, digits even), tracking the parent's current number; a street address still wins as the name.
  - **Mutual-exclusion guard** (`toggleParcelActive` + `lineageConflicts`): activating a parcel auto-deactivates its ancestors AND descendants (a parent covers its children's ground; siblings are disjoint), so a parent and its split children can never both be active.
  - **Schema:** `SITE_MODEL_VERSION` 10 вҶ’ 11 (additive `parentId`; existing records migrate losslessly вҖ” missing = root, unchanged behavior). Fixtures/MAP regenerated.
- **вҸі V210 (live, signed-in + real project data):** on planyr.io, load a real project, split a real county parcel (e.g. Parcel 3, 16.40 ac); confirm Yield reads ~16.4 ac (not ~31.8), the parent shows greyed "В· split" with 3A/3B nested, toggling the parent active deactivates the children, and the whole thing round-trips through cloud save/reload without resurrecting the parent as active. (The pure model + logged-out UI are headless-verified; the signed-in cloud path + owner-data repro are the remaining live gate.)

### B659 вҖ” Sheet reader + file organizer revamp: rotated/offset pages, set-aware titles, left-edge & vertical title blocks, title-first grouping, date-first names `[Doc Review / Library]` (bug вҖ” owner report "they both kinda suckвҖҰ it always messes up in every file") #doc-review #library #files #filing  *(owner chat 2026-07-05 with a screenshot of the GPL Arch IFR review showing "GRAND PORT LOGISTICS" on nearly every rail row + "4 SHEETS В· 44 PAGES"; **B659** = highest real B# across both files (B658) + 1 вҖ” renumbered from a provisional B653 on the origin/main merge-in: a concurrent owner-brief batch took B653вҖ“B658; code comments updated in the same commit. `[x]` **IMPLEMENTED + verified against the owner's REAL Drive sets this session; parks in вҸі Verify (Verify: live вҖ” repro cites real project data) вҶ’ V213.** Every file misread because of five compounding engine gaps; all five are fixed and the fix is retroactive (rail meta is recomputed on every open вҖ” nothing cached to invalidate).
- Verify: live
- Origin: filed 2026-07-05 from chat
- **Root causes found (AUDIT-FIRST, against 6 real sets downloaded from the owner's Drive вҖ” GPL, Jacintoport, Mesa Г—3, Goose Creek ALTA):**
  1. **Page rotation/origin ignored** вҖ” `extractPageItems` read raw PDF text coordinates, but the owner's real files are stored rotated (GPL **180В°**, Mesa mech/site + GC ALTA **270В°**) or origin-shifted (Jacintoport MediaBox at вҲ’1296,вҲ’864), so every zone/band/title/number read looked at the wrong part of the page. Now every run is mapped through the **viewport transform** (what a human sees), any rotation/origin.
  2. **No cross-page signal** вҖ” the title block prints the PROJECT NAME/client/architect stamps LARGER than the sheet title, so the per-page "tallest line" pick returned "GRAND PORT LOGISTICS" on every sheet. New pure module `src/shared/files/sheetTitleSet.js`: per-page ranked `titleCandidates` + a set-level pass (`refineSheetTitles`) that demotes candidates repeating across вүҘ45% of pages (identity stamps) unless they carry a drawing-type word (tiled-run titles), and hard-drops the app's own KNOWN project names/aliases/addresses (`projectStopTexts`; wired in DocReview rail, Stitcher, via `readSheets({stopTexts})`).
  3. **Left-edge & vertical title blocks unreadable** вҖ” Powers Brown-style blocks (the GPL architect) put the number top-corner at 2Г— any type and run titles VERTICALLY. `detectTitleBlock` now knows **left** bands; `reconstructLines` reconstructs **rotated runs as columns** (true reading order, CCW bottomвҶ’top) and fuses **glyph-stacked** pseudo-vertical strings (the Mesa "O I C I 119641 T E" gibberish вҶ’ real lines); wrapped multi-line titles join (incl. across interleaved small cells); a spatial **label-anchored number read** takes the code item NEAREST a "SHEET NUMBER/SHEET NO./DWG NO." caption (content-order joins read the plot timestamp "6/23/2026" as sheet "6"); whole-page prominent-code last resort (вүҘ1.5Г— everything else) for blocks that print the number outside every strip.
  4. **Identity/stamp rows could win as titles** вҖ” new rejections: firm rows (INC/LLC/вҖҰARCHITECTS/вҖҰENGINEERING/вҖҰPLATTING endings), phones/web/email, "Suite N"/street addresses/city-state-zip/lone-state cells, TBPE/TBPLS registrations, "(A) PROJECT FOR вҖҰ"/"PREPARED FOR вҖҰ", the TX interim-review stamp ("PRELIMINARY вҖ” NOT FOR CONSTRUCTIONвҖҰ / CURRENT AS OFвҖҰ"), data-field rows ("SITE AREA : 29.17 AC"), textual dates, mostly-single-letter shreds, and a leading glued sheet-code ("C-2 TOPO SURVEY I" вҶ’ "TOPO SURVEY I").
  5. **Item-first grouping collapsed distinct sheets** вҖ” 44 arch pages sharing item "Architectural" with consecutive numbers became "4 SHEETS". `groupKey` is now **title-first** (with `tileBaseTitle` stripping trailing tile counters "III"/"AREA 2"/"(1 OF 4)" so real tiles still chain); the coarse item is only the no-title fallback; rail/tray labels (`displayTitle`) now show the sheet's OWN title.
- **Organizer half (Library):** list sorts by the DOCUMENT's date (`docRecency` вҖ” issue/revision date first, upload time tiebreak; "latest revision on top" was a lie under updatedAt-sorting), auto-names are **date-first** matching the owner's own convention (`composeTitle`/server `composeFiledName` вҶ’ "2026.06.20 Katy Grand - Grading Plan"), rows show the captured **sheet number/range badge** (toFileFact now carries sheet_number/sheet_title), and a typed re-file discipline normalizes case-insensitively onto the canonical DISCIPLINES list (no more typo-minted duplicate subcategory nodes).

### B644 вҖ” Scheduler embed: first COLD boot throws `Cannot read properties of null (reading 'projects')` + the loader overlay exceeds the 6s backstop (self-recovers) (Г—2) `[Scheduler / robustness]` (bug вҖ” first-paint hardening) #scheduler  *(Cowork live verification 2026-07-03, from V153; minted **B644** = highest real B# across both files (B643) + 1)*
`[x]` **IMPLEMENTED + headless-verified 2026-07-05; parks in вҸі Verify (Verify: live вҖ” timing/race class) вҶ’ V211.** Original report: the FIRST cold SiteвҶ’Schedule switch on planyr.io threw a one-time `вҡ пёҸ This view failed to load вҖ” Cannot read properties of null (reading 'projects')` (~10.5s overlay, self-recovered on re-nav).
- Verify: live
- Recurrence: 2026-07-05 вҖ” owner repro (chat "NEW-5", DEDUPE-FIRST fold вҖ” same error string, same first-paint null-`projects` read): create a project via **Start blank вҶ’ Schedule tab** вҶ’ the same error renders **behind the connect-a-schedule modal**. Deterministic (not only the cold race); expected a clean empty state only.
- **Root cause (pinned by a live sandbox repro, not a guess):** NOT the render path вҖ” the `if (!data) return <loader/>` gate was already sound. The **shellвҶ’iframe nav bridge** (`planar:nav-select` / `nav-select-by-site` / `nav-link` / `nav-create-linked` / `nav-dashboard` / `nav-new` / rename / delete in `public/sequence/index.html`) queues `setData(d => вҖҰ)` functional updaters when the shell announces the active project on a tab switch; before the async `hs-v1` load resolves `d` is **null**, and React runs the queued updater INSIDE the next `useState` mount вҖ” `Object.values(d.projects || {})` throws and lands App in the error boundary. Cold boot = the race version (the bridge message beats the slow cloud load); fresh project = the deterministic version (no schedule linked, load still pending). Captured stack: updater вҶ’ `Object.useState` вҶ’ `App`. The prior "sandbox can't boot the embed" blocker is stale вҖ” the repro serves the embed's CDN deps from local copies via request interception (see the harness).
- **Fix shipped (minimal, matches the in-file `planar:view-set` precedent):** one early gate in the nav-bridge handler вҖ” drop `planar-shell` messages until `latestData.current` exists (the shell re-posts nav intents on every tab switch and retries `nav-request`, so an early drop self-heals the moment the load lands вҖ” the already-documented pre-load no-op behavior, now applied to every branch) вҖ” plus null guards in the three bridge-called helpers (`addProject` / `renameProject` / `deleteProject`) so a future caller can't regress the class.
- **Sandbox-verified 2026-07-05:** `ui-audit/verify-b644-fresh-null.mjs` (new, self-contained вҖ” fetches the four CDN deps once via curl, serves them by request interception): pre-fix it reproduces the exact owner error + stack; post-fix it PASSES (embed renders, zero null-`projects` errors). `jsxcheck-sequence` OK В· build green.

### B672 (Г—2) вҖ” Element-level sync, phase 3/5: realtime read path + rejoin refetch (read cutover; blob frozen) `[Site Planner]` (feature) #site-planner #persistence  *(owner brief 2026-07-06, arrived as "NEW-3"; minted **B672** вҖ” see B671's renumber note. Branch `claude/site-elements-schema-sync-4p2x5b`.)*
`[x]` **IMPLEMENTED this session; parks in вҸі Verify (Verify: live вҖ” cross-tab propagation is a multi-session timing class) вҶ’ V229.** Each open site now subscribes to its `site_elements` rows and applies changes LIVE; with the edit lock still on, a read-only tab updates in real time. This is also the READ CUTOVER: signed-in loads come from rows + a slim header, and the whole-doc blob is FROZEN (`sites.data_backup` = the ~30-day rollback copy).
- Verify: live
- Origin: filed 2026-07-06 from chat
- **Recurrence (2026-07-07, from the Cowork V229 live run вҖ” re-opened, FIXED same session, back to вҸі Verify):**
  **V229 #5 FAILED with a reproduced LOST UPDATE (data-loss class).** Repro: session B's realtime socket
  dropped (`pfSupabase.realtime.disconnect()`), A edits an element (rev 9вҶ’10), B rejoins вҶ’ the DB ends up
  clobbered back to B's stale geometry at rev 11; reproduced twice. **Root cause вҖ” the refetch-replace
  stale-reconcile race:** after `eng.seed(freshRows)` the old `refetchReplace` reconciled against
  `stateRef.current`, which still holds the PRE-replace canvas (setState hadn't rendered) вҖ” on a
  socket-dropped tab that canvas is genuinely stale, so the diff committed OLD geometry as valid
  rev-guarded updates on top of the fresh revs. (#4 passed because a hidden tab still receives events;
  only a dropped socket leaves the canvas stale.) Compounding hole: `flush()` clears the dirty map
  up-front, so the batch IN FLIGHT was invisible to both `applyRemoteRow` and the refetch substitution.
  **Fix (this session):** `refetchReplace` now reconciles against EXACTLY the substituted collections it
  just placed (rows вҲӘ pending local edits), never `stateRef`; it defers wholesale while `busyRef` is live;
  the engine tracks `inflightKeys` during a flush вҖ” in-flight commits are protected like dirty everywhere
  (`applyRemoteRow` keeps local + adopts rev; `dirtyEntries()` includes them so the refetch substitution
  keeps a mid-commit edit; `reconcile` skips re-enqueueing data already on the wire; shadow revs stay
  monotonic when an ok result lands after a newer remote rev was adopted; an identical incoming row is
  adopted silently and drops a duplicate queued write). 6 new unit tests pin the exact #5 sequence +
  in-flight invariants (`test/elementSync.test.js`, "refetch-replace safety"). **Re-run V229 #5 live with
  true DevTools offline** (the Cowork run's disconnect() only severed realtime, not the RPC path вҖ” DevTools
  offline exercises the queued-commit + rejoin path end-to-end).
  - *Watch note (Observation B, same run):* two transient paint freezes were seen under automation-driven
    load; nothing reproduced organically. No action вҖ” watch during the V229 re-run; escalate to its own B#
    only if it shows up under human use.
  - *Related churn fixed same session (Observation A):* the autosave pushed a content-identical slim header
    on every element edit вҖ” each push bumped `sites.version` and CAS-ping-ponged every other tab (a heal per
    edit; noise, and it masked #5's mechanism). `cloudUpsert` now skips a push whose header content is
    unchanged (`headerSig` вҖ” the slim header minus `updatedAt`; baseline seeded from `cloudList`, advanced on
    every successful push, cleared on delete/user-switch; the unload keepalive shares the skip). Trade-off,
    accepted: `sites.updated_at` advances only on REAL header changes (meta/settings/overlays) вҖ” element
    recency lives on the `site_elements` rows. +3 headerSig tests in `test/headerSlim.test.js`.
- **Realtime read path:** one channel per open site (`postgres_changes` filtered to `site_id`); the apply is idempotent per row (`applyRemoteRow`: incoming.rev must BEAT the shadow rev, so our own committed echoes are no-ops); a tombstoned row removes the element; a row for a locally-dirty element keeps LOCAL data and adopts the remote rev (its commit re-targets the fresh row). Remote applies buffer mid-gesture (never yank the canvas mid-drag). **Full refetch + REPLACE on every join/rejoin + tab wake** (visibilitychange) вҖ” never trust event gaps; dirty entries substitute back in; value-identical replaces keep state references (an idle wake re-trues nothing, saves nothing). A failed refetch changes nothing and retries (B54 discipline). No-realtime fallback: a plain fetch still seeds + replaces once, so writes work even if WebSockets are blocked.
- **Header slimming (same commit):** `slimForCloud` strips the 5 vector collections + marks `elementsInRows: true`; `mergePulledSites` understands slim rows (local elements kept вҖ” empty вү  deleted; header-only re-push signature вҖ” no perma-push; a slim row's stale `deletedIds` are excluded from the union so they can never drop a row-restored element).
- **Kill list executed:** the B459 thin-clobber guard + `siteContent`/`siteTombs` baselines + `noteLocalContent` (a slim header would always read as "thinned"; element safety now lives in per-row rev guards); doc-level `cloudConflict` state + the blocking "changed in another session вҖҰ Take over editing" banner (a stale header CAS now SELF-HEALS inside `cloudUpsert` вҖ” refetch the version, re-push once; the B455/B460/B558/B596 false-conflict class is retired BY ARCHITECTURE); the cloud-active storage-event union fold (signed-out keeps it). `deletedIds` refinement: element ids are reconciled against live rows on every refetch (an id with a live row is purged вҖ” rows are deletion-canonical), and it keeps serving header-side collections + signed-out mode.
- **DB executed via Supabase MCP:** backfill re-run captured the phase-1вҶ’3 gap (els 496вҶ’523 вҖ” real owner edits); found + fixed a guard edge (the boot re-push can rewrite blob CONTENT, e.g. the v12 `z` normalization, without advancing `updatedAt` вҶ’ the update guard is now `<=`, engine rows stay strictly newer and untouched); fidelity after heal: **27/28 sites byte-identical, 1 site's rows strictly AHEAD of its blob** (rev 19, server-stamped 400ms after the last blob snapshot вҖ” the healthy dual-write case, rows-canonical). `data_backup` frozen for all 28 sites (`db/site_elements_freeze.sql`).
- **e2e seeds** now explode fixture sites into rows (seed.sql + seed-fixtures.sql), so seeded fixtures open under the rows-canonical read path.
- **Verified here (sandbox):** lint 0 В· 2,835 tests (+19: `elementApply` matrix incl. the composite-key twin case, `headerSlim` merge/no-perma-push/stale-tombstone cases; `cloudThinGuard.test.js` retired with its guard) В· build green В· headless smoke 3/3 (signed-out planner unaffected вҖ” engine + channel are cloud-active-only).
- **вҸі V229 (live, two signed-in sessions):** see VERIFICATION.md вҖ” cross-tab <2s propagation, rejoin refetch, tab-wake re-true, and the no-conflict-banner regression. Folded into the consolidated Cowork runbook (docs/COWORK-ELEMENT-SYNC-LIVE.md, lands with B674).

### B673 вҖ” Element-level sync, phase 4/5: loud-conflict surface + delete/edit matrix `[Site Planner]` (feature) #site-planner #ui #persistence  *(owner brief 2026-07-06, arrived as "NEW-4"; minted **B673** вҖ” see B671's renumber note. Branch `claude/site-elements-schema-sync-4p2x5b`.)*
`[x]` **IMPLEMENTED this session; parks in вҸі Verify (Verify: live вҖ” conflict paths are two-session timing) вҶ’ V230.** No overwrite is ever silent: both sides of a per-element collision get a toast naming who changed what, with **Show** (zoom-to-element + select) or **Restore** riding along. Whole-element granularity, last-write-wins, no field merging вҖ” non-blocking BY DESIGN because nothing is lost.
- Verify: live
- Origin: filed 2026-07-06 from chat
- **The matrix (pure, unit-tested вҖ” `lib/conflictToasts.js`):** edit-vs-edit вҶ’ the losing tab re-commits (LWW) and reads "вҹЁelementвҹ© was also just edited by вҹЁnameвҹ© вҖ” your version was kept"; the overwritten tab (a foreign rev inside the ~15s authored window) reads "вҹЁnameвҹ© changed вҹЁelementвҹ© you just edited вҖ” their version is showing" (over-trigger inside the window is by design). Editing a deleted element вҶ’ tombstone hit вҶ’ the deletion shows on canvas + "вҹЁelementвҹ© was deleted by вҹЁnameвҹ©" with **Restore** (a new `restore` op: clears the tombstone, writes your data, new rev; racing a live row adopts THEIRS + a follow-up notice). Deleting a just-edited element вҶ’ the delete re-applies at the fresh rev (delete wins, silent for the deleter); the editor's side gets the removal + supersede notice. Create-vs-create вҶ’ impossible by construction (per-tab salted ids, B591) вҖ” telemetry assert only. Remote changes OUTSIDE the window stay quiet (that's just live sync).
- **Attribution (`lib/editorNames.js`):** self-uid вҶ’ "you (another window)"; teammates via the SECURITY DEFINER `list_team_members` roster RPC (profiles RLS is own-row-only), cached per site session; roster miss вҶ’ "a teammate", never blank. Element labels via `describeElement` вҖ” buildings by their on-canvas display number ("Building 3"), others by type/kind.
- **Toast component (`src/shared/ui/Toast.jsx`, reusable):** non-blocking stack, auto-dismiss 8s with HOVER-HOLD (mouse over pauses the timer), optional action button, cap 4 + "+n more", `role="status"`, theme tokens only, solid fill + weight (never faded text; amber accent bar вҖ” red stays reserved for genuine alert). MODULE-SCOPE components.
- **zoom-to-element:** new `zoomToElement(kind, id)` frames the element's bbox (the frameToActiveParcels math over `featBBox`) + selects it вҖ” no per-element zoom existed before.
- **Verified here (sandbox):** lint 0 В· 2,852 tests (+17: the full matrix mapping both sides + quiet passes, restore op ok/conflict flows, name resolver cache/self/fallback, describeElement, toast pure helpers) В· build green В· headless smoke 3/3 (signed-out untouched).
- **вҸі V230 (live, two signed-in sessions):** same-element race both-sides toasts with correct names, restore end-to-end, delete-vs-edit supersede notice. Until B674 removes the lock, same-browser tabs can't race (read-only gate) вҖ” the matrix is reachable cross-DEVICE now and fully same-browser after B674; folded into the consolidated Cowork runbook (docs/COWORK-ELEMENT-SYNC-LIVE.md, lands with B674).
- **2026-07-07 Cowork run: NOT faithfully exercised** вҖ” both sessions were the same account, so the named-toast halves ("вҹЁnameвҹ© changedвҖҰ") and the team-roster attribution never fired ("you (another window)" is the only reachable label same-account). Still вҸі pending a run with a SECOND account on a team-shared site (the one owner-side input вҖ” see OWNER-TODO).
- DEDUPE-FIRST: net-new (see B670); B455 (Done) demanded loud+BLOCKING conflict handling under the old whole-doc model вҖ” this is its per-element successor, non-blocking because LWW + both sides told + Restore means nothing is lost.

### B714 вҖ” Sharing a project silently REVERTS: any ordinary save from the owner's open tab overwrote `sites.team_id` back to null, locking the collaborator out `[Site Planner / Review / teams В· RLS]` (bug вҖ” data-integrity class) #site-planner #persistence #auth  *(owner live repro 2026-07-08 with the Cowork session: right-clicked Goose Creek вҶ’ Share to michael.butler@hillwood.com вҶ’ the site APPEARED on the test account, then broke вҖ” red cloud, elements gone after reload, no conflict toasts. Cowork's DB forensics found team "HIP Houston" + both members present but 0 sites linked, and filed it as "Share never sets team_id" (their NEW-1). First minted **B692**, then **B714** вҖ” BOTH taken by concurrent sessions on successive merge-ins of `origin/main` (B692 = the husk-parcel root-cause fix; B714 = dock-high truck-court pricing); settled as **B714** = highest B# across both files (B714) + 1.)*
`[x]` **IMPLEMENTED + unit-verified this session; parks in вҸі Verify (Verify: live вҖ” the share round-trip is two-account/auth-only) вҶ’ V244.** Sharing now survives every save: the sharing pointer can only be changed by the explicit Share/unshare action, never by a content autosave.
- Verify: live
- Origin: filed 2026-07-08 from the owner's live session (Cowork brief NEW-1 + NEW-2)
- **AUDIT-FIRST вҖ” the reported diagnosis was half right; the code reality is worse and explains everything.** `lib/sharing.js` DOES set `sites.team_id` correctly (UPDATE by `group_id`; the row's `group_id` is populated; the owner passes the rehome-guard trigger) вҖ” that's why the site initially appeared on the test account. The real bug: **every ordinary content push re-stamped `team_id` from the client's IN-MEMORY model** (`cloudUpsertCore` + `keepaliveCloudPush` for `sites`; `upsertReviewCore` + `keepaliveFlushReview` for `doc_reviews`; `upsertFileFacts` for `file_facts`, whose filing callers never even carry a teamId вҶ’ hard `null`). The owner's open Goose Creek tab predated the share, so its next autosave wrote `team_id: null` вҖ” silently unsharing (the B486 rehome guard deliberately exempts the OWNER, so it never fired; a signed-in tab never re-reads the store, so it never learned the share happened). Timeline confirmed live: team created 2026-06-24, both members admins; the site row rewritten to v61 the same night with `team_id` back at null.
- **Fix вҖ” team_id is write-isolated to the sharing flow, everywhere:** `siteRowFor` / `reviewRowFor` (new pure row builders) OMIT `team_id` on every update вҖ” CAS autosaves and unload keepalives physically cannot carry the sharing pointer anymore; a brand-NEW row (first insert) still stamps the model's teamId so a plan/review created inside a shared project is born shared. `upsertFileFacts` sends `team_id` only when a caller explicitly provides one (the plain-upsert update leg then leaves the column untouched). `slimForCloud` additionally strips `teamId`/`ownerId` from the stored jsonb вҖ” the columns are the single source of truth, overlaid onto models at read time (`cloudList`/`loadReview`), and this keeps `headerSig` share-neutral so the B672 unchanged-header skip still works on shared sites.
- **Cowork's NEW-2 (realtime RLS "leak") вҖ” resolved by the same root cause, no leak.** The test account saw the owner's building move BEFORE its lockout because at that moment the site WAS legitimately shared (team_id set, RLS satisfied); the subsequent autosave-revert then produced the red cloud (writes rejected) and empty reload (reads rejected). Supabase `postgres_changes` enforces RLS per-subscriber, and the un-share also kills the subscription's row visibility. The V244 run includes a sanity check on a genuinely-unshared site.
- **Follow-on (small, filed not lost):** a file FILED into an already-shared project lands with `team_id null` (fact-row callers don't know the project's team) until the next re-share stamps it вҖ” pre-existing behavior, now explicit. Fix later by resolving the project's live team at filing time.
- **Verified here (sandbox):** 8-test `test/teamShareGuard.test.js` pins the rule for every writer (update rows carry NO team_id key; insert rows inherit; slim jsonb stripped; headerSig share-neutral) В· full suite green В· build green.
- **Data heal (prod):** the owner's intended share re-applied after deploy вҖ” `sites.team_id = 454aa114вҖҰ(HIP Houston)` restored on group `smqfy48tlk9j` (Goose Creek) via MCP SQL (rehome-guard trigger safely bypassed for the one maintenance UPDATE; re-verified after).
- **вҸі V244 (live, two accounts вҖ” both already exist):** see VERIFICATION.md.
- DEDUPE-FIRST: net-new (no prior B# covers the share flow or team_id write-isolation); DISTINCT from the concurrent **B692** (husk-parcel model sanitize вҖ” the other half of the same live run's findings); B486 (Done) is the non-owner rehome guard this bug walked around by BEING the owner. The same owner brief's NEW-3 = **B690**/**B692** (render guard + root cause, both shipped) and NEW-4 = **B672 (Г—2)** (fixed + merged 2026-07-08) вҖ” the live session ran on build 40884e6, which predates those fixes; no new numbers minted for them.

### B641 вҖ” Outfall intelligence: flowline + design-tailwater sourcing `[Site Planner / Stormwater]` (feature вҖ” umbrella; tier-2/3 screening slice SHIPPED with B636вҖ“B640)  *(owner brief 2026-07-03, arrived as "NEW-6" roadmap; owner then asked for the tractable slice in-session; first filed **B634**, RENUMBERED to **B641** on merge-in of `origin/main` вҖ” concurrent sessions took B629вҖ“B635; B641 = highest real B# across both files (B640) + 1. Code/harness keep the provisional B629-batch labels вҖ” see the B636 note in BACKLOG-DONE.md.)*
`[ ]` Source the receiving system's flowline + design-storm tailwater to move Regime-A coverage (B632) from assumption to sourced band. Confidence tiers: **(1) HCFCD effective HEC-RAS model extraction** (channel-bottom + WSEL by storm at the nearest cross-section вҖ” highest confidence; BLOCKER: external model acquisition + a HEC-RAS parser, own workstream), **(2) LiDAR ditch-bottom for open ditches** (3DEP) вҖ” вң… **first slice shipped 2026-07-03**: `screenOutfall()` samples a 3DEP cross-profile through the nearest HCFCD channel unit (`ditchStats` invert/bank/depth) and renders the value-of-information line in the Regime-A banner ("assumed shallow outfall vs measured ditch depth вҖ” here's what to pull to confirm"); never auto-credited, **(3) storm-sewer GIS inverts** (COH `UN_Stormwater` already wired; HGL/surcharge caveat: a deep pipe invert with a high hydraulic grade line is Regime B, not A вҖ” needs invert-field probing on the geogimstest host), **(4) adjacent-plan OCR via Document Review** (BLOCKER: rides auto-filing). Output pattern stays value-of-information: "assumed shallow outfall = X% coverage; if the receiving channel is deep and unsubmerged, ~Y% вҖ” worth Z sf; here's what to pull to confirm." This is the substance of the `docs/ROADMAP.md` Tier-1 "storm outfall" item (annotated there; the rate-rules half = B636).

### B623 вҖ” User-editable schedule conventions (working week, holidays, month/year roll behavior) `[Scheduler]` (feature)  *(owner-dropped 2026-07-02 as "NEW-3", filed to Later/Roadmap by owner instruction вҖ” do NOT build until moved up; provisionally NEW-3/"B617", renumbered **B623** on the `origin/main` merge-in that took B615вҖ“B620; B623 = highest real B# across both files (B622) + 1)*
`[ ]` **Roadmap вҖ” sequence AFTER B621/B622 (the duration model + finish lock, in-code labels `B615`/`B616`) prove out.** A settings surface letting the user edit the schedule's own date conventions, extending the existing holiday-selection UI to also cover: (a) the **working week** вҖ” e.g. enable **6-day weeks** (B621 hard-codes the week to 5 working days; this makes it editable), and optionally (b) the **month/year roll behavior** (the plain-forward roll B621 fixed). Reasonable extension since holiday selection already exists (`ensureHolidays` / `HOLIDAY_SET` in `public/sequence/index.html`). **Same loud/visible discipline as the rest of the schedule:** the working week and roll direction silently change every derived date, so any change must **re-run cascade and SURFACE the shifted dates** (before/after diff, same discipline as B621's migration), never move them quietly. Depends on the B621 duration model (week-factor is currently the hard-coded `DUR_WD_FACTOR.w = 5` + the weekend test inside `addBD`/`workdaysBetween`/`rollForwardToWorkday` вҖ” those become the parameterized seam) and the B622 conflict-surfacing pattern (reuse the banner/row-flag). **Do NOT parameterize the week inside B621** вҖ” that was deliberately deferred here.

### B371 вҖ” GIS screening cache Phase 2: regional Houston-metro snapshot / offline pre-cache `[Site Planner / Analysis]` (feature) вҖ” Phase 2 of B367  *(filed 2026-06-22; minted **B371**)*
`[ ]` **Later (gated behind B367 Phase 1, which shipped).** Phase 1 (B367) keeps the last-good answer per parcel+layer and never blanks a layer on a transient outage. Phase 2 is the owner's "cache most of Houston" idea: a **regional pre-cache/snapshot** of the Houston-metro source layers (+ a coverage mask), refreshed on a schedule, so a **never-seen** parcel with no features resolves **offline** to "No <layer> mapped (source vintage <date>)" instead of waiting on (or failing) a live query. Heavier вҖ” needs storage (a Supabase table or a static snapshot) + a refresh job + a coverage mask so "no features in the snapshot" is trustworthy only inside the cached extent. Deferred deliberately behind Phase 1 per the brief; pick up once Phase 1 proves out in the field.

### B340 вҖ” Auto-assembly CV tails behind the B335вҖ“B339 seams `[Doc Review / Stitch]` (feature) вҖ” the hard minority  *(filed 2026-06-21 as the deferred remainder of the B335вҖ“B339 batch; minted **B340** вҖ” a hot `main` took B325вҖ“B334)*
`[ ]` The B335вҖ“B339 headline flow (drop a set вҶ’ auto-group вҶ’ auto-stitch вҶ’ crop вҶ’ auto-calibrate) is **shipped + verified** for the common case вҖ” CAD vector PDFs with a real text layer. (Scanned-sheet **OCR** was the 4th tail and is now **DONE вҶ’ B352**, shipped + verified this session.) Three computer-vision tails remain, deferred behind clean injectable seams because each needs vector-graphics analysis we can't yet headless-verify вҖ” and the manual-Align safety net already covers them:
  1. **Graphic scale-bar reading (B339 tail)** вҖ” when there's no stated scale text, measure the drawn scale bar to set `ftPerUnit`. Needs vector-graphics/CV analysis, not text.
  2. **Geometric edge-line match (B337 middle fallback)** вҖ” when match-line *labels* are missing, match the cut geometry across two sheets' edges. Today, label-less sheets correctly drop to the 2-point manual Align **pre-seeded** with detected seam endpoints (the spec's final safety net, already wired) вҖ” this is the CV step between labels and manual.
  3. **Legend symbol-union (B338 tail)** вҖ” extract each sheet's graphical legend entries and union them into the pinned Composite key (today the key lists the grouped plan + auto-scale; the crop + pinned panel ship). Needs symbol/vector extraction.
> Each is gated behind a seam exactly like the app's other not-yet-provisioned heavy compute (the AI title-block reader, the APS converter). Pick up when there's a way to verify (a CV pass we can headless-check). Coupled to the вҳ… north-star "map вҶ’ drawings вҶ’ latest set."
>
> **AMENDMENT 2026-07-03 (owner pulled the CV tails into active scope, Cowork brief) вҖ” the PURE ENGINES for all three now ship + are unit-tested; the browser EXTRACTION + live verification remain.** These reduce manual-Align on *real* plan sets; they do **NOT** fix the JACINTOPORT schedule-set wall (that was B630вҖ“B633). What landed this session:
> 1. **Graphic scale-bar reading** вҖ” `src/shared/files/scaleBarRead.js` (`readScaleBar` + `clusterBars`/`ticksNearBar`/`tickLinearity`), wired fail-open via `sheetRead.scaleBarCalibration` as a fallback in `groupCalibration` (stated scale still wins). Reads a drawn bar's geometry + tick labels вҶ’ `feetPerUnit`; only applies on a high-confidence, feet-unit read, never over a stated/manual cal.
> 2. **Geometric edge-line match** вҖ” `src/shared/files/edgeGeomMatch.js` (`fitEdgeLine` PCA/total-least-squares + `orderEndpoints` + `matchSeamEdges`), wired fail-open via `autoStitch.seamEndpointsFor` (prefers a drawn seam's geometry over the rectangle edge; improve-only, keeps the pre-seeded 2-point net). The vector path complementing the raster fitter (`matchLineFit.js`, B413).
> 3. **Legend symbol-union** вҖ” `src/shared/files/legendUnion.js` (`unionLegendEntries` + `legendFromPlaced`), wired into the Stitcher Composite key (rendered only when non-empty).
> **STILL OPEN (why this stays here):** each engine consumes geometry that a **browser vector/CV extractor must supply** вҖ” the `scaleBar` fact, per-sheet `seamGeom`, and per-sheet `legendEntries` вҖ” and **nothing populates those seams yet**, so all three are **dormant / zero behavior change today** (dormant exactly like the OCR/APS seams). None can be headless-verified вҶ’ the extraction + real-browser proof on the owner's sets is **V201**. Fail open throughout; never present a topology-only placement as "aligned."

### B256 вҖ” Scheduler recompute is O(nВІ); will lag past ~500 tasks `[Scheduler / perf]` (task)  *(orig "P2"; minted **B256**)*
`[ ]` `cascadeDates`/`rollupParentDates` re-filter the task list repeatedly on each edit; `depLines` calls `tasks.indexOf` inside its loop; `rolledHealthMap`/`progressMap` recurse with `.filter`. Fine at the current ~180 tasks; will start to feel laggy past ~500. Fix: build an `id вҶ’ index` map and a `parent вҶ’ children[]` map once per recompute and reuse them вҖ” behaviour-preserving. **Verify** every task's start/end/duration is byte-identical before/after on the real production dataset. Gated by board size вҶ’ Later until a board actually grows that large.

### B257 вҖ” Optional: instant cross-device "newer version" banner via Supabase realtime `[Scheduler / cloud]` (feature)  *(orig "B2 follow-up"; minted **B257**)*
`[ ]` The version-stamp guard + 20s polling already ship and work (the "newer version вҖ” Reload" banner appears within ~20s). Optional upgrade: enable Supabase **realtime** on the Scheduler data table and subscribe to row changes so the banner shows within ~1s; keep the 20s poll as a fallback if the channel drops. Needs a one-line SQL toggle on the Supabase project (owner/dashboard) вҖ” an external dependency вҖ” and it's polish, not a bug, so it sits in Later.

### B258 вҖ” Incremental cleanup of inline styles / inner-defined helpers `[Scheduler / code health]` (task)  *(orig "P4"; minted **B258**)*
`[ ]` Standing, opportunistic cleanup: as each Scheduler panel is touched for other work, hoist any helper components defined inside their parent to module scope (props-only) and lift repeated literal `style={{вҖҰ}}` objects to module consts; memoize hot row renderers. B247 (the `Field` hoist) was the user-visible tip of this. Do it incrementally as code is touched вҖ” explicitly **not** one big sweep (UI must stay identical at each step), which is why it lives here rather than as a discrete Open task.

### B259 вҖ” Scheduler off in-browser Babel вҶ’ a real build step `[Scheduler / build]` (project)  *(orig "P1/M1"; minted **B259**)*
`[ ]` The entire Scheduler (`public/sequence/index.html`, ~9.6k lines) is compiled by `@babel/standalone` in the browser on every load. Project-level work: move to a real build step / modularize. **Entangled** with the file's ability to save its own data back into itself (the File System Access auto-save rewrites the `<script id="planar-data">` block inside the HTML), so any change must preserve self-save. Plan deliberately; not required for any other Scheduler item. Deferred by design.

### B272 вҖ” Rule out a main-thread stall from non-Workerized heavy parsing `[Core / Site Planner]` (bug, low priority)  *(owner-dropped 2026-06-20 via chat; arrived as "NEW-2"; minted **B272** вҖ” secondary hypothesis to B271)*
`[ ]` Secondary hypothesis for the same "unclickable canvas" symptom: heavy CAD/PDF parse (or other compute) running on the **main thread** instead of a Web Worker, jamming the tab. **Investigated 2026-06-20 (B271 session):** PDF parsing already runs **off** the main thread вҖ” PDF.js uses its worker (a separate `pdf.worker` chunk in the build); DWGвҶ’DXF conversion is a **backend** (`/server`) concern, never in the browser. The reported incident's symptom (a frozen grab/hand cursor + clicks swallowed, with **no** Chrome "Page Unresponsive вҖ” Wait/Exit" prompt) is the signature of stuck pointer state, not a CPU stall, and is fully explained + fixed by **B271**. **No actionable main-thread-stall bug found.** Per the owner's note this drops to **low priority** now that B271 resolves the lockout вҖ” kept here (not closed) so it stays on the radar. **Escalate only** if an actual stall is ever observed: then instrument long-task timing, reproduce with a large drawing, and move any straggler heavy compute into a Worker per the standing architecture rule.

- **Enforced merge gate via GitHub branch protection** (the settings half of **B63**): require a PR + a passing build check + "branch up to date before merging" on `main`, plus repo auto-merge. On the **private** repo this only *enforces* on a paid plan (GitHub Pro+); on Free the rules save but don't block вҖ” so B63's branch вҶ’ PR вҶ’ green discipline is the backstop until then. Keep it a manual owner toggle rather than granting the Claude Code app admin rights on a credential-bound repo.

- **B150 вҖ” Wire dedicated county appraisal districts (CADs) for the Austin & DFW metros** `[Site Planner / map]` (feature) вҖ” *filed 2026-06-18 as a later-feature note (owner asked to park it).* Today only **Harris / Fort Bend / Chambers** have dedicated CADs in `lib/counties.js` (`COUNTIES` + `COUNTIES_MAP`). Austin (Travis/**TCAD**, Williamson, Hays) and DFW (Tarrant/**TAD**, Dallas/**DCAD**, Denton, Collin) parcels currently work **only via the statewide TxGIO fallback** (B137) вҖ” coverage is complete (verified: Travis 835K, Tarrant 757K, Dallas 694K, Williamson/Hays/Denton/Collin all present) and returns owner/situs/market-value/acreage, but the statewide copy can **lag** a county's live CAD and carries a **thinner field set** than the district's own service. Wire each county's dedicated CAD (verify it publishes a reachable, **CORS-clean** parcel service first вҖ” same vetting as the ETJ sources; some counties publish cleanly, some don't) so Austin/DFW get the same first-class, most-current parcel/appraisal data Houston has via HCAD/FBCAD; add per-county bbox routing to `candidateCountiesForPoint` as each lands.
  - **Bundle the county-mislabel fix:** a parcel in a non-configured county is presently tagged `chambers` (the statewide source's key) because the **B36(a)** `countyAtPoint` relabel only maps to the 3 wired CAD keys вҖ” so an Austin/DFW lot saves with the wrong `county`. Record the **true** county name even when no dedicated CAD is wired (cosmetic today; matters for the saved Site Model + which jurisdiction defaults show).
  - Coupled to **B11 / B13 / B36 / B137** (the county-resolution theme). **Not urgent** вҖ” the statewide fallback keeps Austin/DFW functional meanwhile; pick up when the owner is actively working those metros (start with Travis, Tarrant, Dallas).
